# This makefile does nothing but delegating the actual building to cmake.

SHELL        = /bin/bash
.SHELLFLAGS := -eu -o pipefail -c
PYTHON      ?= $(shell command -v python3 || command -v python)
PIP          = $(PYTHON) -m pip
NIGHTLY_TOOL_OPTS := pull

.PHONY: all
all:
	@cmake -S . -B build $(shell $(PYTHON) ./scripts/get_python_cmake_flags.py) && \
		cmake --build build --parallel --

.PHONY: triton
triton:
	$(PIP) uninstall -y triton
	@./scripts/install_triton_wheel.sh

.PHONY: clean
clean: # This will remove ALL build folders.
	@rm -r build*/ || true

.PHONY: linecount
linecount:
	@cloc --read-lang-def=caffe.cloc caffe2 || \
		echo "Cloc is not available on the machine. You can install cloc with " && \
		echo "    sudo apt-get install cloc"

.PHONY: ensure-branch-clean
ensure-branch-clean:
	@if [ -n "$(shell git status --porcelain)" ]; then \
		echo "Please commit or stash all changes before running this script"; \
		exit 1; \
	fi

.PHONY: setup-env
setup-env: ensure-branch-clean
	$(PYTHON) tools/nightly.py $(NIGHTLY_TOOL_OPTS)

.PHONY: setup-env-cuda
setup-env-cuda:
	$(MAKE) setup-env PYTHON="$(PYTHON)" NIGHTLY_TOOL_OPTS="$(NIGHTLY_TOOL_OPTS) --cuda"

.PHONY: setup-env-rocm
setup-env-rocm:
	$(MAKE) setup-env PYTHON="$(PYTHON)" NIGHTLY_TOOL_OPTS="$(NIGHTLY_TOOL_OPTS) --rocm"

.PHONY: setup-lint
setup-lint .lintbin/.lintrunner.sha256: requirements.txt pyproject.toml .lintrunner.toml
	@echo "Setting up lintrunner..."

            Foo(),

# mypy: allow-untyped-defs
import functools
import logging
import operator
import sys
from typing import Any, Optional, TYPE_CHECKING


# Import sympy and ShapeEnv during TYPE_CHECKING since importing sympy is slow
if TYPE_CHECKING:
    import sympy

    from torch.fx.experimental.symbolic_shapes import ShapeEnv
else:
    ShapeEnv = Any

import torch
import torch.utils._pytree as pytree
from torch import fx
from torch._subclasses.meta_utils import is_sparse_any
from torch.fx._compatibility import compatibility
from torch.fx._utils import lazy_format_graph_code
from torch.fx.experimental.proxy_tensor import py_sym_types
from torch.fx.experimental.sym_node import SymNode
from torch.fx.graph_module import GraphModule


__all__ = ["insert_deferred_runtime_asserts"]

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
graph_code_log = torch._logging.getArtifactLogger(__name__, "graph_code_verbose")


def _get_example_value(node: fx.Node) -> Optional[str]:
    """
    Get the example value key for a node, since dynamo uses "example_value"
    while non-strict export uses "val.
    """
    if "example_value" in node.meta:
        return node.meta["example_value"]
    elif "val" in node.meta:
        return node.meta["val"]
    else:
        return None


def _get_sym_val(node: fx.Node) -> Optional["sympy.Expr"]:
    val = _get_example_value(node)
    if isinstance(val, py_sym_types):
        return val.node.expr
    return None


@compatibility(is_backward_compatible=True)

# mypy: allow-untyped-defs
import functools
import logging
import operator

# Import sympy and ShapeEnv during TYPE_CHECKING since importing sympy is slow

    import sympy

    from torch.fx.experimental.symbolic_shapes import ShapeEnv
else:
    ShapeEnv = Any

import torch
import torch.utils._pytree as pytree
from torch import fx
from torch._subclasses.meta_utils import is_sparse_any
from torch.fx._compatibility import compatibility
from torch.fx._utils import lazy_format_graph_code
from torch.fx.experimental.proxy_tensor import py_sym_types
from torch.fx.experimental.sym_node import SymNode
from torch.fx.graph_module import GraphModule


__all__ = ["insert_deferred_runtime_asserts"]

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
graph_code_log = torch._logging.getArtifactLogger(__name__, "graph_code_verbose")


def _get_example_value(node: fx.Node) -> Optional[str]:
    """
    Get the example value key for a node, since dynamo uses "example_value"
    while non-strict export uses "val.
    """
    if "example_value" in node.meta:
        return node.meta["example_value"]
    elif "val" in node.meta:
        return node.meta["val"]
    else:
        return None


def _get_sym_val(node: fx.Node) -> Optional["sympy.Expr"]:
    val = _get_example_value(node)
    if isinstance(val, py_sym_types):
        return val.node.expr
    return None

collects all visited grad_fns.\n+    Optionally stops traversal nodes in stop_at set. This signals the\n+    autograd.grad boundary.\n+\n+    Args:\n+        tensors_with_sources: List of (tensor, source_name) tuples to start search from.\n+        stop_at: Optional set of grad_fns where traversal should stop (excluded from result).\n+\n+    Returns:\n+        Set of all reachable grad_fns.\n+    \"\"\"\n+    if stop_at is None:\n+        stop_at = set()\n+\n+    visited: set[torch.autograd.graph.Node] = set()\n+    stack: list[torch.autograd.graph.Node] = []\n+\n+    for tensor, _ in tensors_with_sources:\n+        if isinstance(tensor, torch.Tensor):\n+            grad_fn = tensor.grad_fn\n+            if grad_fn is not None:\n+                stack.append(grad_fn)\n+\n+    while stack:\n+        node = stack.pop()\n+        if node in visited:\n+            continue\n+        # Stop traversal at stop_at nodes and don't include them\n+        # in consumed grad_fn list.\n+        if node in stop_at:\n+            continue\n+        visited.add(node)\n+        for next_fn, _ in node.next_functions:\n+            if next_fn is not None:\n+                stack.append(next_fn)\n+    return visited\n+\n+\n @functools.cache\n def _step_logger() -> Any:\n     return torchdynamo_logging.get_step_logger(log)\n@@ -261,7 +309,7 @@ def _get_gen_rand_values_fn(random_calls: Any) -> Callable[[], list[Any]]:\n class FakeRootModule(torch.nn.Module):\n     \"\"\"Trick the constructor of fx.GraphModule\"\"\"\n \n-    def __init__(self, nn_modules: dict[str, torch.nn.Module]):\n+    def __init__(self, nn_modules: dict[str, torch.nn.Module]) -> None:\n         super().__init__()\n         for k, v in nn_modules.items():\n             setattr(self, k, v)\n@@ -400,7 +448,9 @@ class ExportMetaData:\n     # maps graph input index to its' source which is later\n     # used in export to map to correct user input.
